hu_in01,385,247,5	script	普斯特#D	97,{

	mes "[普斯特]";
	mes "Hey, uh...";
	mes "I'm in the middle";
	mes "of something here.";
	close;

OnInit:
	disablenpc "普斯特#D";
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc "普斯特#D";
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer100000:
	disablenpc "普斯特#D";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;
	
OnSweat:
	emotion e_swt;
	end;

OnEffect:
	specialeffect 174;
	end;

}

	if(hg_herb == 1) {

		next;
		mes "[普斯特]";
		mes "哦? 药吗? 那个是... 虽然 我父亲正躺在 病榻上...但反正是定期会 发生的事情，";
		mes "所以不必 立即投药，时间一过 就会自然而然痊愈的";
		next;
		mes "[普斯特]";
		mes "因此不用太担心，我父亲他也已经 习以为常没关系的，重要的是要享受这和平、尽情玩乐才会更有益的?";
		next;
		switch( select( "我有要转告的话:嗯，当然更有益了" )){
		case 1:
			mes "[艾轮的 声音]";
			mes "我会将我亲爱的儿子普斯特，专门把他贬抑村落姑娘娜X小姐所写下收录的株株字迹~";
			mes "字迹之笔记本交给X荷小姐，让她尝尝所谓的真正爱情!!";
			next;
			mes "[普斯特]";
			mes "呜哇好厉害!!! 一模一样!!!讲这话之前... 这是攸关性命的问题，";
			mes "呼呼... 我得跑一趟了，请你在这段时间好好照顾父亲，不要让他发生什么意外...";
			next;
			mes "[普斯特]";
			mes "呜噢噢噢!!! 孝子 Mode ON! 孝机器战士 普斯特V!!! 8身合体 孝子铁金刚!!! Go Go Go!!!";
			next;
			mes "[" +strcharinfo(0)+ "]";
			mes "(...)";
			mes "(我要先去找艾轮...)";
			set hg_herb,2;
			close;
		break;
		case 2:
			mes "[" +strcharinfo(0)+ "]";

			mes "(我的灵魂过于单纯，)";
			mes "(装作不知道离开吧...) ";
			close;
		break;
		}
	}
	else if(hg_herb > 1) {
		mes "[普斯特]";
		mes "玩~吧玩吧，年轻时尽量玩吧，";
		mes "不玩会后悔~父亲曾说 ";
		mes "要尽情享受风流快活~";
		next;
		mes "[普斯特]";
		mes "哈哈哈哈阿... 现在就要过去了... ";
		mes "就要过去了...";
		close;

		mes "[普斯特]";
		mes "享受吧!";
		next;

		mes "继续享受吧!";
		next;

		mes "尽情享受吧!";
		close;

	disablenpc "#DrawerOpener";
	end;

	initnpctimer;
	end;

	enablenpc "上层 抽屉#Second";
	disablenpc "上层 抽屉#First";
	end;

	enablenpc "上层 抽屉#First";
	disablenpc "上层 抽屉#Second";
	disablenpc "#DrawerOpener";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

hu_fild06,168,359,3	script	Moks Mushrooms#Mush1	111,{

	if(hg_tre > 9 && hg_tre < 15)
	{
		mes "- You found mushrooms that is as big as your palm. -";
		next;
		switch( select( "Gather them.","Pass." ) )
		{
		case 1:
			mes "- You decided to gather the mushrooms. -";
			next;
			mes "- *Snip Snip* -";
			next;
			mes "- *Snip Snip* -";
			mes "- *Snip Snip* -";
			next;
			mes "- *Snip Snip* -";
			mes "- *Snip Snip* -";
			mes "- *Snip Snip* -";
			specialeffect2 71;
			next;
			if(rand(1,5) > 4)
			{
				mes "- You were being clumsy and broke the mushrooms. You have failed in gathering the mushrooms. -";
				specialeffect2 194;
				close;
			}
			mes "- You have successfully gathered mushrooms. -";
			specialeffect2 364;
			set hg_tre,hg_tre+1;
			if(hg_tre == 11)
				mes "Collected Moks Mushroom Solution: 1ea ";
			else if(hg_tre == 12)
				mes "Collected Moks Mushroom Solution: 2ea ";
			else if(hg_tre == 13)
				mes "Collected Moks Mushroom Solution: 3ea ";
			else if(hg_tre == 14)
				mes "Collected Moks Mushroom Solution: 4ea ";
			else if(hg_tre == 15)
				mes "Collected Moks Mushroom Solution: 5ea ";
			initnpctimer;
			disablenpc "Moks Mushroom#Mush1";
			close;
		break;
		case 2:
			mes "- You decided to pass by them. -";
			close;
		break;
		}
	}
	else if(hg_tre == 15)
	{
		mes "["+strcharinfo(0)+"]";
		mes "I think that this will do.";
		close;
	}

OnTimer20000:
	enablenpc "Moks Mushroom#Mush1";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

}

			}

				mes "[西雷托]";

				mes "很好的麻吉朋友，因此";

				mes "冷掉就不好吃了";
				set hg_odeng,1;
				getitem 584,1; //Skewer soup
				close;
			}
			else if(@randvar == 2) {
				mes "[西雷托]";
				mes "我的粉丝中有一位叫做 玫宛，";
				mes "他以前作生意时我曾帮过忙，";
				mes "从此之后他就成了我的粉丝，";
				mes "一直帮我到现在，食物冷掉";
				mes "就不好吃了，请赶快";
				mes "送去吧~";
				set hg_odeng,2;
				getitem 584,1; //Skewer soup
				close;
			}
			else if(@randvar == 3)
			{
				mes "[西雷托]";
				mes "这次是我的室友拉尤麻小姐，";
				mes "她很会修理家中的家具，";
				mes "另外她只要看到盗虫就会";
				mes "吓得花容失色，";
				mes "麻烦你快点~";
				set hg_odeng,3;
				getitem 584,1; //Skewer soup
				close;
			}
			else if(@randvar == 4)
			{
				mes "[西雷托]";
				mes "这次是以吹毛求疵而盛名有贵族病的";
				mes "艾乐詹先生，虽然他有点难伺候，";
				mes "不过却是个好人，";
				mes "若不快点送去，等食物凉了，";
				mes "他也许会斥责你的";
				set hg_odeng,4;
				getitem 584,1; //Skewer soup
				close;
			}
		break;
		case 2:
			mes "[西雷托]";
			mes "是喔，你是想尝尝黑轮的";
			mes "味道是吗，我知道了，特别";
			mes "为你做好吃的黑轮汤，";
			mes "一人份100金币";
			next;
			switch( select( "买:不买" ) )
			{
			case 1:
				if(Zeny > 99)
				{
					mes "[西雷托]";
					mes "谢谢你，请享用";
					set Zeny,Zeny-100;
					getitem 584,1; //Skewer soup
					close;
				}
				else
				{
					mes "[西雷托]";
					mes "你所拥有的金币不足";
					mes "所以不能吃黑轮汤";
					close;
				}
			break;
			case 2:
				mes "[西雷托]";
				mes "是吗? 好可惜，若改变注意时，";
				mes "再过来尝尝吧";
				close;
			break;
			}
		break;
		case 3:

function	script	Func_MilkCow	{


	mes "^3355FFThis giant magic comb was";
	mes "specially ordered from Geffen's";
	mes "Magic Academy. It is designed";
	mes "to operate after inserting";
	mes "3 Concentration Potions";
	mes "into its special slots.^000000";
	next;
	mes "^3355FFOnce you place your";
	mes "3 Concentration Potions";
	mes "into the comb, it begins";
	mes "to chime, and Booboo the";
	mes "cow beings to express her^FFFFFF ^3355FF feelings in the center of Hugel.^000000";
	delitem 645,3;
	soundeffect ""+getarg(0)+"",0;
	next;
	soundeffect ""+getarg(0)+"",0;
	mes "^3355FFNow it's time for you";
	mes "to brush Mrs.布乌布乌.";
	mes "Depending on her mood,";
	mes "you need to brush her a";
	mes "certain number of times.^000000";
	next;
	input @cowbrush;
	if (@cowbrush != getarg(1))
	{
		soundeffect "taming_fail.wav",0;
		mes "^3355FFAwwww...";
		mes "Mrs.布乌布乌 looks";
		mes "so disappointed. She";
		mes "looks like she wants";
		mes "to close herself off";
		mes "from the rest of the world...^000000";
		close;
	}
	soundeffect "cow_06.wav",0;
	mes "^3355FFMrs.布乌布乌";
	mes "seems fairly content,";
	mes "and is singing a serenade.^000000";
	next;
	soundeffect "cow_06.wav",0;
	set @cowsong2,rand(1,6);
	mes "[Mrs. Booboo]";
	if (@cowsong2 == 1)
	{
		mes "^ff0000Brr~ Brrboo~ Boobooboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBrrrrrr~ Booboo~ Boorrboo~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Booruboorubrr~ Rrrrboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrr~ Booboorrrr~ Boobooru~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Boobooboo~ Rururu~ Booruboorub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBoo! B! Boo~~~^000000";
	}
	else if (@cowsong2 == 2)
	{
		mes "^ff0000Brr~ Brrboo~ Boobooboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrururu~ Booboo~ Boorrboo~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Booruboorubrr~ Rrrrboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrr~ Booboorrrr~ Boobooru~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Boobooboo~ Rururu~ Booruboorub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBoo! B! Boo~~~^000000";
	}
	else if (@cowsong2 == 3)
	{
		mes "^ff0000Brr~ Brrbrr~ Boobooboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBrrrrrr~ Booboo~ Boorrboo~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Booruboorubrr~ Rurub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrr~ Booboorrrr~ Boobooru~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Boobooboo~ Rururu~ Booruboorub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBoo! B! Boo~^000000";
	}
	else if (@cowsong2 == 4)
	{
		mes "^ff0000Brr~ Brrbrr~ Boobooboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBrrrrrr~ Booboo~ Boorrboo~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Booruboorubrr~ Rrrrboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrr~ Booboorrrr~ Bbrrrr~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Boobooboo~ Rururu~ Booruboorub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBoo! B! Boo~^000000";
	}
	else if (@cowsong2 == 5)
	{
		mes "^ff0000Brr~ Brrbrr~ Boobooboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBrrrrrr~ Booboo~ Boorrboo~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Booruboorubrr~ Rrrrboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrr~ Booboorrrr~ Boobooru~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Bbb~ Rururu~ Booruboorub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBoo! B! Boo~^000000";
	}
	else if (@cowsong2 == 6)
	{
		mes "^ff0000Brr~ Brrbrr~ Boobooboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBrrrrrr~ Booboo~ Boorrboo~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Booruboorubrr~ Rrrrboo~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffRrrr~ Booboorrrr~ Boobooru~^000000";
		mes "^ff0000Boobooboo~ Rururu~ Booruboorub~^000000";
		mes "^0000ffBoo! Boo! Boo~^000000";
	}
	next;
	mes "^3355FFHurry, respond to Booboo's song! Look for the word that is slightly";
	mes "different than Booboo's normal";
	mes "song in 布陆普's notes, and then tell her the correct world without";
	mes "the tilde character (''~'').^000000";
	next;
	if(@cowsong2 == 1) set @cowsong$,"Brrbrr";
	else if(@cowsong2 == 2) set @cowsong$,"Brrrrrr";
	else if(@cowsong2 == 3) set @cowsong$,"Rrrrboo";
	else if(@cowsong2 == 4) set @cowsong$,"Boobooru";
	else if(@cowsong2 == 5) set @cowsong$,"Boobooboo";
	else if(@cowsong2 == 6) set @cowsong$,"B";
	input @cowanswer$;
	if (@cowanswer$ == @cowsong$)
	{
		soundeffect "tming_success.wav",0;
		mes "^3355FFSuccess!";
		mes "Mrs.布乌布乌";
		mes "is quite happy, and";
		mes "you were able to milk";
		mes "her. Now, you should";
		mes "report to 库陆培.^000000";
		if(hg_milk == 12) set hg_milk,13;
		else set hg_milk,8;
		close;
	}
	soundeffect "taming_fail.wav",0;
	mes "^3355FFUh oh...";
	mes "Mrs.布乌布乌 is starting";
	mes "to snort violently! She seems";
	mes "pretty angry with you, so you";
	mes "better get away for now...^000000";
	close;
}
